createRemoteLogManager(listenerInfo: ListenerInfo): Option[RemoteLogManager] = {\n    if (config.remoteLogManagerConfig.isRemoteStorageSystemEnabled) {\n      val listenerName = }\n\n  override def shutdown(timeout: Duration): Unit = {\n    if (!maybeChangeStatus(STARTED, SHUTTING_DOWN)) return\n    try {\n      val deadline = time.milliseconds() + timeout.toMillis\n      info(\"shutting down\")\n\n      if (config.controlledShutdownEnable) {\n        if (replicaManager != null)\n          replicaManager.beginControlledShutdown()\n\n        if (lifecycleManager != null) {\n          lifecycleManager.beginControlledShutdown()\n          try {\n            val controlledShutdownTimeoutMs = deadline - time.milliseconds()\n            lifecycleManager.controlledShutdownFuture.get(controlledShutdownTimeoutMs, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS)\n          } catch {\n            case _: TimeoutException =>\n              error(\"Timed out waiting for the controller to approve controlled shutdown\")\n            case e: Throwable =>\n              error(\"Got unexpected exception waiting for controlled shutdown future\", e)\n          }\n        }\n      }\n      if (lifecycleManager != null)\n        lifecycleManager.beginShutdown()\n\n      // Stop socket server to stop accepting any more connections and requests.\n      // Socket server will be shutdown towards the end of the sequence.\n      if (socketServer != null) {\n        CoreUtils.swallow(socketServer.stopProcessingRequests(), this)\n      }\n      metadataPublishers.forEach(p => sharedServer.loader.removeAndClosePublisher(p).get())\n      metadataPublishers.clear()\n      if (dataPlaneRequestHandlerPool != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(dataPlaneRequestHandlerPool.shutdown(), this)\n      if (dataPlaneRequestProcessor != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(dataPlaneRequestProcessor.close(), this)\n      authorizerPlugin.foreach(Utils.closeQuietly(_, \"authorizer plugin\"))\n\n      /**\n       * We must shutdown the scheduler early because otherwise, the scheduler could touch other\n       * resources that might have been shutdown and cause exceptions.\n       * For example, if we didn't shutdown the scheduler first, when LogManager was closing\n       * partitions one by one, the scheduler might concurrently delete old segments due to\n       * retention. However, the old segments could have been closed by the LogManager, which would\n       * cause an IOException and subsequently mark logdir as offline. As a result, the broker would\n       * not flush the remaining partitions or write the clean shutdown marker. Ultimately, the\n       * broker would have to take hours to recover the log during restart.\n       */\n      if (kafkaScheduler != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(kafkaScheduler.shutdown(), this)\n\n      if (transactionCoordinator != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(transactionCoordinator.shutdown(), this)\n\n      if (groupConfigManager != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(groupConfigManager.close(), this)\n      if (groupCoordinator != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(groupCoordinator.shutdown(), this)\n      if (shareCoordinator != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(shareCoordinator.shutdown(), this)\n\n      if (assignmentsManager != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(assignmentsManager.close(), this)\n\n      if (replicaManager != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(replicaManager.shutdown(), this)\n\n      if (alterPartitionManager != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(alterPartitionManager.shutdown(), this)\n\n      if (forwardingManager != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(forwardingManager.close(), this)\n\n      if (clientToControllerChannelManager != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(clientToControllerChannelManager.shutdown(), this)\n\n      if (logManager != null) {\n        val brokerEpoch = if (lifecycleManager != null) lifecycleManager.brokerEpoch else -1\n        CoreUtils.swallow(logManager.shutdown(brokerEpoch), this)\n      }\n\n      // Close remote log manager to give a chance to any of its underlying clients\n      // (especially in RemoteStorageManager and RemoteLogMetadataManager) to close gracefully.\n      remoteLogManagerOpt.foreach(Utils.closeQuietly(_, \"remote log manager\"))\n\n      if (quotaManagers != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(quotaManagers.shutdown(), this)\n\n      if (socketServer != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(socketServer.shutdown(), this)\n\n      Utils.closeQuietly(brokerTopicStats, \"broker topic stats\")\n      Utils.closeQuietly(sharePartitionManager, \"share partition manager\")\n\n      if (persister != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(persister.stop(), this)\n\n      isShuttingDown.set(false)\n\n      if (lifecycleManager != null)\n        CoreUtils.swallow(lifecycleManager.close(), this)\n\n      CoreUtils.swallow(config.dynamicConfig.clear(), this)\n      Utils.closeQuietly(clientMetricsManager, \"client metrics manager\")\n      sharedServer.stopForBroker()\n      info(\"shut down completed\")\n    } catch {\n      case e: Throwable =>\n        fatal(\"Fatal error during broker shutdown.\", e)\n        throw e\n    } finally {\n      maybeChangeStatus(SHUTTING_DOWN, SHUTDOWN)\n    }\n  }\n\n  override def isShutdown(): Boolean = {\n    status == SHUTDOWN || status == SHUTTING_DOWN\n  }\n\n  override def awaitShutdown(): Unit = {\n    lock.lock()\n    try {\n      while (true) {\n        if (status == SHUTDOWN) return\n        awaitShutdownCond.awaitUninterruptibly()\n      }\n    } finally {\n      lock.unlock()\n    }\n  }\n\n  override def boundPort(listenerName: ListenerName): Int = socketServer.boundPort(listenerName)\n\n}\n","numLines":864,"startLine":1,"totalLines":864}}}

36→import scala.collection.mutable\n    37→import scala.jdk.CollectionConverters._\n    38→\n    39→/**\n    40→ * The broker lifecycle manager owns the broker state.\n    41→ *\n    42→ * Its inputs are messages passed in from other parts of the broker and from the\n    43→ * controller: requests to start up, or shut down, for example. Its output are the broker\n    44→ * state and various futures that can be used to wait for broker state transitions to\n    45→ * occur.\n    46→ *\n    47→ * The lifecycle manager handles registering the broker with the controller, as described\n    48→ * in KIP-631. After registration is complete, it handles sending periodic broker\n    49→ * heartbeats and processing the responses.\n    50→ *\n    51→ * This code uses an event queue paradigm. Modifications get translated into events, which\n    52→ * are placed on the queue to be processed sequentially. As described in the JavaDoc for\n    53→ * each variable, most mutable state can be accessed only from that event queue thread.\n    54→ * In some cases we expose a volatile variable which can be read from any thread, but only\n    55→ * written from the event queue thread.\n    56→ */\n    57→class BrokerLifecycleManager(\n    58→  val config: KafkaConfig,\n    59→  val time: Time,\n    60→  val threadNamePrefix: String,\n    61→  val logDirs: Set[Uuid],\n    62→  val shutdownHook: () => Unit = () => {}\n    63→) extends Logging {\n    64→\n    65→  private def logPrefix(): String = {\n    66→    val builder = new StringBuilder(\"[BrokerLifecycleManager\")\n    67→    builder.append(\" id=\").append(config.nodeId)\n    68→    builder.append(\"] \")\n    69→    builder.toString()\n    70→  }\n    71→\n    72→  val logContext = new LogContext(logPrefix())\n    73→\n    74→  this.logIdent = logContext.logPrefix()\n    75→\n    76→  /**\n    77→   * The broker id.\n    78→   */\n    79→  private val nodeId = config.nodeId\n    80→\n    81→  /**\n    82→   * The broker rack, or null if there is no configured rack.\n    83→   */\n    84→  private val rack = config.rack\n    85→\n    86→  /**\n    87→   * How long to wait for registration to succeed before failing the startup process.\n    88→   */\n    89→  private val initialTimeoutNs =\n    90→    MILLISECONDS.toNanos(config.initialRegistrationTimeoutMs.longValue())\n    91→\n    92→  /**\n    93→   * The broker incarnation ID.  This ID uniquely identifies each time we start the broker\n    94→   */\n    95→  val incarnationId: Uuid = Uuid.randomUuid()\n    96→\n    97→  /**\n    98→   * A future which is completed just as soon as the broker has caught up with the latest\n    99→   * metadata offset for the first time.\n   100→   */\n   101→  val initialCatchUpFuture: CompletableFuture[Void] = new CompletableFuture[Void]()\n   102→\n   103→  /**\n   104→   * A future which is completed when the broker is unfenced for the first time.\n   105→   */\n   106→  val initialUnfenceFuture: CompletableFuture[Void] = new CompletableFuture[Void]()\n   107→\n   108→  /**\n   109→   * A future which is completed when controlled shutdown is done.\n   110→   */\n   111→  val controlledShutdownFuture: CompletableFuture[Void] = new CompletableFuture[Void]()\n   112→\n   113→  /**\n   114→   * The broker epoch, or -1 if the broker has not yet registered.  This variable can only\n   115→   * be written from the event queue thread.\n   116→   */\n   117→  @volatile private var _brokerEpoch = -1L\n   118→\n   119→  /**\n   120→   * The current broker state.  This variable can only be written from the event queue\n   121→   * thread.\n   122→   */\n   123→  @volatile private var _state = BrokerState.NOT_RUNNING\n   124→\n   125→  /**\n   126→   * A thread-safe callback function which gives this manager the current highest metadata\n   127→   * offset.  This variable can only be read or written from the event queue thread.\n   128→   */\n   129→  private var _highestMetadataOffsetProvider: () => Long = _\n   130→\n   131→  /**\n   132→   * True only if we are ready to unfence the broker.  This variable can only be read or\n   133→   * written from the event queue thread.\n   134→   */\n   135→  private var readyToUnfence = false\n   136→\n   137→  /**\n   138→   * Map of accumulated offline directories. The value is true if the directory couldn't be communicated\n   139→   * to the Controller.\n   140→   * This variable can only be read or written from the event queue thread.\n   141→   */\n   142→  private var offlineDirs = mutable.Map[Uuid, Boolean]()\n   143→\n   144→  /**\n   145→   * True if we sent an event queue to the active controller requesting controlled\n   146→   * shutdown.  This variable can only be read or written from the event queue thread.\n   147→   */\n   148→  private var gotControlledShutdownResponse = false\n   149→\n   150→  /**\n   151→   * Whether or not this broker is registered with the controller quorum.\n   152→   * This variable can only be read or written from the event queue thread.\n   153→   */\n   154→  private var registered = false\n   155→\n   156→  /**\n   157→   * True if a request has been sent and a response or timeout has not yet been processed.\n   158→   * This variable can only be read or written from the event queue thread.\n   159→   */\n   160→  private var communicationInFlight = false\n   161→\n   162→  /**\n   163→   * True if we should schedule the next communication immediately. This is used to delay\n   164→   * an immediate scheduling of a communication event if one is already in flight.\n   165→   * This variable can only be read or written from the event queue thread.\n   166→   */\n   167→  private var nextSchedulingShouldBeImmediate = false\n   168→\n   169→  /**\n   170→   * True if the initial registration succeeded.  This variable can only be read or\n   171→   * written from the event queue thread.\n   172→   */\n   173→  private var initialRegistrationSucceeded = false\n   174→\n   175→  /**\n   176→   * The cluster ID, or null if this manager has not been started yet.  This variable can\n   177→   * only be read or written from the event queue thread.\n   178→   */\n   179→  private var _clusterId: String = _\n   180→\n   181→  /**\n   182→   * The listeners which this broker advertises.  This variable can only be read or\n   183→   * written from the event queue thread.\n   184→   */\n   185→  private var _advertisedListeners: ListenerCollection = _\n   186→\n   187→  /**\n   188→   * The features supported by this broker.  This variable can only be read or written\n   189→   * from the event queue thread.\n   190→   */\n   191→  private var _supportedFeatures: util.Map[String, VersionRange] = _\n   192→\n   193→  /**\n   194→   * The channel manager, or null if this manager has not been started yet.  This variable\n   195→   * can only be read or written from the event queue thread.\n   196→   */\n   197→  private var _channelManager: NodeToControllerChannelManager = _\n   198→\n   199→  /**\n   200→   * The broker epoch from the previous run, or empty if the epoch is not found.\n   201→   */\n   202→  @volatile private var previousBrokerEpoch: OptionalLong = OptionalLong.empty()\n   203→\n   204→  /**\n   205→   * The event queue.\n   206→   */\n   207→  private[server] val eventQueue = new KafkaEventQueue(time,\n   208→    logContext,\n   209→    threadNamePrefix + \"lifecycle-manager-\",\n   210→    new ShutdownEvent())\n   211→\n   212→  /**\n   213→   * Start the BrokerLifecycleManager.\n   214→   *\n   215→   * @param highestMetadataOffsetProvider Provides the current highest metadata offset.\n   216→   * @param channelManager                The NodeToControllerChannelManager to use.\n   217→   * @param clusterId                     The cluster ID.\n   218→   * @param advertisedListeners           The advertised listeners for this broker.\n   219→   * @param supportedFeatures             The features for this broker.\n   220→   * @param StartupEvent(highestMetadataOffsetProvider,\n   231→      channelManager, clusterId, advertisedListeners, supportedFeatures))\n   232→  }\n   233→\n   234→  def setReadyToUnfence(): CompletableFuture[Void] = {\n   235→    eventQueue.append(new SetReadyToUnfenceEvent())\n   236→    initialUnfenceFuture\n   237→  }\n   238→\n   239→  /**\n   240→   * Propagate directory failures to the controller.\n   241→   * @param directory The ID for the directory that failed.\n   242→   */\n   243→  def propagateDirectoryFailure(directory: Uuid, timeout: Long): Unit = {\n   244→    eventQueue.append(new OfflineDirEvent(directory))\n   245→    // If we can't communicate the offline directory to the controller, we should shut down.\n   246→    eventQueue.scheduleDeferred(\"offlineDirFailure\",\n   247→      new DeadlineFunction(time.nanoseconds() + MILLISECONDS.toNanos(timeout)),\n   248→      new OfflineDirBrokerFailureEvent(directory))\n   249→  }\n   250→\n   251→  def resendBrokerRegistration(): Unit = {\n   252→    eventQueue.append(new ResendBrokerRegistrationEvent())\n   253→  }\n   254→\n   255→  private class ResendBrokerRegistrationEvent extends EventQueue.Event {\n   256→    override def run(): Unit = {\n   257→      registered = false\n   258→      scheduleNextCommunicationImmediately()\n   259→    }\n   260→  }\n   261→\n   262→  def brokerEpoch: Long = _brokerEpoch\n   263→\n   264→  def state: BrokerState = _state\n   265→\n   266→  private class BeginControlledShutdownEvent extends EventQueue.Event {\n   267→    override def run(): Unit = {\n   268→      _state match {\n   269→        case BrokerState.PENDING_CONTROLLED_SHUTDOWN =>\n   270→          info(\"Attempted to enter pending controlled shutdown state, but we are \" +\n   271→          \"already in that state.\")\n   272→        case BrokerState.RUNNING =>\n   273→          info(\"Beginning controlled shutdown.\")\n   274→          _state = BrokerState.PENDING_CONTROLLED_SHUTDOWN\n   275→          // Send the next heartbeat immediately in order to let the controller\n   276→          // begin processing the controlled shutdown as soon as possible.\n   277→          scheduleNextCommunicationImmediately()\n   278→\n   279→        case _ =>\n   280→          info(s\"Skipping controlled shutdown because we are in state ${_state}.\")\n   281→          beginShutdown()\n   282→      }\n   283→    }\n   284→  }\n   285→\n   286→  /**\n   287→   * Enter the controlled shutdown state if we are in RUNNING state.\n   288→   * Or, if we're not running, shut down immediately.\n   289→   */\n   290→  def beginControlledShutdown(): Unit = {\n   291→    eventQueue.append(new BeginControlledShutdownEvent())\n   292→  }\n   293→\n   294→  /**\n   295→   * Start shutting down the BrokerLifecycleManager, but do not block.\n   296→   */\n   297→  def beginShutdown(): Unit = {\n   298→    eventQueue.beginShutdown(\"beginShutdown\")\n   299→  }\n   300→\n   301→  /**\n   302→   * Shut down the BrokerLifecycleManager and block until all threads are joined.\n   303→   */\n   304→  def close(): Unit = {\n   305→    beginShutdown()\n   306→    eventQueue.close()\n   307→  }\n   308→\n   309→  private class SetReadyToUnfenceEvent extends EventQueue.Event {\n   310→    override def run(): Unit = {\n   311→      readyToUnfence = true\n   312→      scheduleNextCommunicationImmediately()\n   313→    }\n   314→  }\n   315→\n   316→  private class OfflineDirEvent(val dir: Uuid) extends EventQueue.Event {\n   317→    override def run(): Unit = {\n   318→      if (offlineDirs.isEmpty) {\n   319→        offlineDirs = mutable.Map(dir -> false)\n   320→      } else {\n   321→        offlineDirs += (dir -> false)\n   322→      }\n   323→      if (registered) {\n   324→        scheduleNextCommunicationImmediately()\n   325→      }\n   326→    }\n   327→  }\n   328→\n   329→  private class OfflineDirBrokerFailureEvent(offlineDir: Uuid) extends EventQueue.Event {\n   330→    override def run(): Unit = {\n   331→      if (!offlineDirs.getOrElse(offlineDir, false)) {\n   332→        error(s\"Shutting down because couldn't communicate offline log dir $offlineDir with controllers\")\n   333→        shutdownHook()\n   334→      }\n   335→    }\n   336→  }\n   337→\n   338→  private class StartupEvent(highestMetadataOffsetProvider: () => Long,\n   339→                     channelManager: NodeToControllerChannelManager,\n   340→                     clusterId: String,\n   341→                     advertisedListeners: ListenerCollection,\n   342→                     supportedFeatures: util.Map[String, VersionRange]) extends EventQueue.Event {\n   343→    override def run(): Unit = {\n   344→      _highestMetadataOffsetProvider = highestMetadataOffsetProvider\n   345→      _channelManager = channelManager\n   346→      _channelManager.start()\n   347→      _state = BrokerState.STARTING\n   348→      _clusterId = clusterId\n   349→      _advertisedListeners = advertisedListeners.duplicate()\n   350→      _supportedFeatures = new util.HashMap[String, VersionRange](supportedFeatures)\n   351→      eventQueue.scheduleDeferred(\"initialRegistrationTimeout\",\n   352→        new DeadlineFunction(time.nanoseconds() + initialTimeoutNs),\n   353→        new RegistrationTimeoutEvent())\n   354→      sendBrokerRegistration()\n   355→      info(s\"Incarnation $incarnationId of broker $nodeId in cluster $clusterId \" +\n   356→        \"is now STARTING.\")\n   357→    }\n   358→  }\n   359→\n   360→  private def sendBrokerRegistration(): Unit = {\n   361→    val features = new BrokerRegistrationRequestData.FeatureCollection()\n   362→    _supportedFeatures.asScala.foreach {\n   363→      case (name, range) => features.add(new BrokerRegistrationRequestData.Feature().\n   364→        setName(name).\n   365→        setMinSupportedVersion(range.min()).\n   366→        setMaxSupportedVersion(range.max()))\n   367→    }\n   368→    val sortedLogDirs = new util.ArrayList[Uuid]\n   369→    logDirs.foreach(sortedLogDirs.add)\n   370→    sortedLogDirs.sort(new Comparator[Uuid]() {\n   371→      override def compare(a: Uuid, b: Uuid): Int = a.compareTo(b)\n   372→    })\n   373→    val data = new BrokerRegistrationRequestData().\n   374→        setBrokerId(nodeId).\n   375→        setIsMigratingZkBroker(false).\n   376→        setClusterId(_clusterId).\n   377→        setFeatures(features).\n   378→        setIncarnationId(incarnationId).\n   379→        setListeners(_advertisedListeners).\n   380→        setRack(rack.orNull).\n   381→        setPreviousBrokerEpoch(previousBrokerEpoch.orElse(-1L)).\n   382→        setLogDirs(sortedLogDirs)\n   383→    if (isDebugEnabled) {\n   384→      debug(s\"Sending broker registration $data\")\n   385→    }\n   386→    _channelManager.sendRequest(new BrokerRegistrationRequest.Builder(data),\n   387→      new BrokerRegistrationResponseHandler())\n   388→    communicationInFlight = true\n   389→  }\n   390→\n   391→  // the response handler is not invoked from the event handler thread,\n   392→  // so it is not safe to update state here, instead, schedule an event\n   393→  // to continue handling the response on the event handler thread\n   394→  private class BrokerRegistrationResponseHandler extends ControllerRequestCompletionHandler {\n   395→    override def onComplete(response: ClientResponse): Unit = {\n   396→      eventQueue.prepend(new BrokerRegistrationResponseEvent(response, false))\n   397→    }\n   398→\n   399→    override def onTimeout(): Unit = {\n   400→      info(s\"Unable to register the broker because the RPC got timed out before it could be sent.\")\n   401→      eventQueue.prepend(new BrokerRegistrationResponseEvent(null, true))\n   402→    }\n   403→  }\n   404→\n   405→  private class BrokerRegistrationResponseEvent(response: ClientResponse, timedOut: Boolean) extends EventQueue.Event {\n   406→    override def run(): Unit = {\n   407→      communicationInFlight = false\n   408→      if (timedOut) {\n   409→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   410→        return\n   411→      }\n   412→      if (response.authenticationException() != null) {\n   413→        error(s\"Unable to register broker $nodeId because of an authentication exception.\",\n   414→          response.authenticationException())\n   415→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   416→      } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\n   417→        error(s\"Unable to register broker $nodeId because of an API version problem.\",\n   418→          response.versionMismatch())\n   419→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   420→      } else if (response.responseBody() == null) {\n   421→        warn(s\"Unable to register broker $nodeId.\")\n   422→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   423→      } else if (!response.responseBody().isInstanceOf[BrokerRegistrationResponse]) {\n   424→        error(s\"Unable to register broker $nodeId because the controller returned an \" +\n   425→          \"invalid response type.\")\n   426→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   427→      } else {\n   428→        val message = response.responseBody().asInstanceOf[BrokerRegistrationResponse]\n   429→        val errorCode = Errors.forCode(message.data().errorCode())\n   430→        if (errorCode == Errors.NONE) {\n   431→          _brokerEpoch = message.data().brokerEpoch()\n   432→          registered = true\n   433→          initialRegistrationSucceeded = true\n   434→          info(s\"Successfully registered broker $nodeId with broker epoch ${_brokerEpoch}\")\n   435→          scheduleNextCommunicationImmediately() // Immediately send a heartbeat\n   436→        } else {\n   437→          info(s\"Unable to register broker $nodeId because the controller returned \" +\n   438→            s\"error $errorCode\")\n   439→          scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   440→        }\n   441→      }\n   442→    }\n   443→  }\n   444→\n   445→  private def sendBrokerHeartbeat(): Unit = {\n   446→    val metadataOffset = _highestMetadataOffsetProvider()\n   447→    val data = new BrokerHeartbeatRequestData().\n   448→      setBrokerEpoch(_brokerEpoch).\n   449→      setBrokerId(nodeId).\n   450→      setCurrentMetadataOffset(metadataOffset).\n   451→      setWantFence(!readyToUnfence).\n   452→      setWantShutDown(_state == BrokerState.PENDING_CONTROLLED_SHUTDOWN).\n   453→      setOfflineLogDirs(offlineDirs.keys.toSeq.asJava)\n   454→    if (isTraceEnabled) {\n   455→      trace(s\"Sending broker heartbeat $data\")\n   456→    }\n   457→    val handler = new BrokerHeartbeatResponseHandler(offlineDirs.keys)\n   458→    _channelManager.sendRequest(new BrokerHeartbeatRequest.Builder(data), handler)\n   459→    communicationInFlight = true\n   460→  }\n   461→\n   462→  // the response handler is not invoked from the event handler thread,\n   463→  // so it is not safe to update state here, instead, schedule an event\n   464→  // to continue handling the response on the event handler thread\n   465→  private class BrokerHeartbeatResponseHandler(currentOfflineDirs: Iterable[Uuid]) extends ControllerRequestCompletionHandler {\n   466→    override def onComplete(response: ClientResponse): Unit = {\n   467→      eventQueue.prepend(new BrokerHeartbeatResponseEvent(response, false, currentOfflineDirs))\n   468→    }\n   469→\n   470→    override def onTimeout(): Unit = {\n   471→      info(\"Unable to send a heartbeat because the RPC got timed out before it could be sent.\")\n   472→      eventQueue.prepend(new BrokerHeartbeatResponseEvent(null, true, currentOfflineDirs))\n   473→    }\n   474→  }\n   475→\n   476→  private class BrokerHeartbeatResponseEvent(response: ClientResponse, timedOut: Boolean,\n   477→                                             currentOfflineDirs: Iterable[Uuid]) extends EventQueue.Event {\n   478→    override def run(): Unit = {\n   479→      communicationInFlight = false\n   480→      if (timedOut) {\n   481→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   482→        return\n   483→      }\n   484→      if (response.authenticationException() != null) {\n   485→        error(s\"Unable to send broker heartbeat for $nodeId because of an \" +\n   486→          \"authentication exception.\", response.authenticationException())\n   487→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   488→      } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\n   489→        error(s\"Unable to send broker heartbeat for $nodeId because of an API \" +\n   490→          \"version problem.\", response.versionMismatch())\n   491→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   492→      } else if (response.responseBody() == null) {\n   493→        warn(s\"Unable to send broker heartbeat for $nodeId. Retrying.\")\n   494→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   495→      } else if (!response.responseBody().isInstanceOf[BrokerHeartbeatResponse]) {\n   496→        error(s\"Unable to send broker heartbeat for $nodeId because the controller \" +\n   497→          \"returned an invalid response type.\")\n   498→        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   499→      } else {\n   500→        val message = response.responseBody().asInstanceOf[BrokerHeartbeatResponse]\n   501→        val errorCode = Errors.forCode(message.data().errorCode())\n   502→        if (errorCode == Errors.NONE) {\n   503→          val responseData = message.data()\n   504→          currentOfflineDirs.foreach(cur => offlineDirs.put(cur, true))\n   505→          _state match {\n   506→            case BrokerState.STARTING =>\n   507→              if (responseData.isCaughtUp) {\n   508→                info(s\"The broker has caught up. Transitioning from STARTING to RECOVERY.\")\n   509→                _state = BrokerState.RECOVERY\n   510→                initialCatchUpFuture.complete(null)\n   511→              } else {\n   512→                debug(s\"The broker is STARTING. Still waiting to catch up with cluster metadata.\")\n   513→              }\n   514→              // Schedule the heartbeat after only 10 ms so that in the case where\n   515→              // there is no recovery work to be done, we start up a bit quicker.\n   516→              scheduleNextCommunication(NANOSECONDS.convert(10, MILLISECONDS))\n   517→            case BrokerState.RECOVERY =>\n   518→              if (!responseData.isFenced) {\n   519→                info(s\"The broker has been unfenced. Transitioning from RECOVERY to RUNNING.\")\n   520→                initialUnfenceFuture.complete(null)\n   521→                _state = BrokerState.RUNNING\n   522→              } else {\n   523→                info(s\"The broker is in RECOVERY.\")\n   524→              }\n   525→              scheduleNextCommunicationAfterSuccess()\n   526→            case BrokerState.RUNNING =>\n   527→              debug(s\"The broker is RUNNING. Processing heartbeat response.\")\n   528→              scheduleNextCommunicationAfterSuccess()\n   529→            case BrokerState.PENDING_CONTROLLED_SHUTDOWN =>\n   530→              if (!responseData.shouldShutDown()) {\n   531→                info(s\"The broker is in PENDING_CONTROLLED_SHUTDOWN state, still waiting \" +\n   532→                  \"for the active controller.\")\n   533→                if (!gotControlledShutdownResponse) {\n   534→                  // If this is the first pending controlled shutdown response we got,\n   535→                  // schedule our next heartbeat a little bit sooner than we usually would.\n   536→                  // In the case where controlled shutdown completes quickly, this will\n   537→                  // speed things up a little bit.\n   538→                  scheduleNextCommunication(NANOSECONDS.convert(50, MILLISECONDS))\n   539→                } else {\n   540→                  scheduleNextCommunicationAfterSuccess()\n   541→                }\n   542→              } else {\n   543→                info(s\"The controller has asked us to exit controlled shutdown.\")\n   544→                beginShutdown()\n   545→              }\n   546→              gotControlledShutdownResponse = true\n   547→            case BrokerState.SHUTTING_DOWN =>\n   548→              info(s\"The broker is SHUTTING_DOWN. Ignoring heartbeat response.\")\n   549→            case _ =>\n   550→              error(s\"Unexpected broker state ${_state}\")\n   551→              scheduleNextCommunicationAfterSuccess()\n   552→          }\n   553→        } else {\n   554→          warn(s\"Broker $nodeId sent a heartbeat request but received error $errorCode.\")\n   555→          scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n   556→        }\n   557→      }\n   558→    }\n   559→  }\n   560→\n   561→  private def scheduleNextCommunicationImmediately(): Unit = {\n   562→      scheduleNextCommunication(0)\n   563→  }\n   564→\n   565→  private def scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure(): Unit = {\n   566→    nextSchedulingShouldBeImmediate = false // never immediately reschedule after a failure\n   567→    scheduleNextCommunication(NANOSECONDS.convert(\n   568→      config.brokerHeartbeatIntervalMs.longValue() , MILLISECONDS))\n   569→  }\n   570→\n   571→  private def scheduleNextCommunicationAfterSuccess(): Unit = {\n   572→    scheduleNextCommunication(NANOSECONDS.convert(\n   573→      config.brokerHeartbeatIntervalMs.longValue() , MILLISECONDS))\n   574→  }\n   575→\n   576→  private def scheduleNextCommunication(intervalNs: Long): Unit = {\n   577→    val adjustedIntervalNs = if (nextSchedulingShouldBeImmediate) 0 else intervalNs\n   578→ BrokerHeartbeatResponseEvent(response: ClientResponse, timedOut: Boolean,\n                                             currentOfflineDirs: Iterable[Uuid]) extends EventQueue.Event {\n    override def run(): Unit = {\n      communicationInFlight = false\n      if (timedOut) {\n        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n        return\n      }\n      if (response.authenticationException() != null) {\n        error(s\"Unable to send broker heartbeat for $nodeId because of an \" +\n          \"authentication exception.\", response.authenticationException())\n        scheduleNextCommunicationAfterFailure()\n      } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\n        error(s\"Unable to send broker heartbeat for $nodeId because of an API \" +\n Transitioning from STARTING to RECOVERY.\")\n                _state = BrokerState.RECOVERY\n                initialCatchUpFuture.complete(null)\n              } else {\n                debug(s\"The broker is STARTING. Still waiting to catch up with cluster metadata.\")\n              }\n              // Schedule the heartbeat after only 10 ms so that in the case where\n              // there is no recovery work to be done, we start up a bit quicker.\n              scheduleNextCommunication(NANOSECONDS.convert(10, MILLISECONDS))\n            case BrokerState.RECOVERY =>\n              if (!responseData.isFenced) {\n                info(s\"The broker has been unfenced. Transitioning from RECOVERY to RUNNING.\")\n                initialUnfenceFuture.complete(null)\n                _state = BrokerState.RUNNING\n              } else {\n                info(s\"The broker is in RECOVERY.\")\n              }\n              scheduleNextCommunicationAfterSuccess()\n            case BrokerState.RUNNING =>\n              debug(s\"The broker is RUNNING. false // never immediately reschedule after a failure\n    scheduleNextCommunication(NANOSECONDS.convert(\n      config.brokerHeartbeatIntervalMs.longValue() , MILLISECONDS))\n  }\n\n  private def It is responsible for\n * constructing the controller and/or broker based on the `process.roles`\n * configuration and for managing their basic lifecycle (startup and shutdown).\n *\n */\nclass KafkaRaftServer(\n  config: KafkaConfig,\n  time: Time,\n) extends Server with Logging {\n\n  this.logIdent = s\"[KafkaRaftServer nodeId=${config.nodeId}] \"\n\n  private val (metaPropsEnsemble, bootstrapMetadata) =\n    KafkaRaftServer.initializeLogDirs(config, this.logger.underlying, this.logIdent)\n\n  private val metrics = Server.initializeMetrics(\n    config,\n    time,\n    metaPropsEnsemble.clusterId().get()\n  )\n\n  private val sharedServer = new SharedServer(\n    config,\n    metaPropsEnsemble,\n    time,\n    metrics,\n    CompletableFuture.completedFuture(QuorumConfig.parseVoterConnections(config.quorumConfig.voters)),\n    QuorumConfig.parseBootstrapServers(config.quorumConfig.bootstrapServers),\n    new StandardFaultHandlerFactory(),\n    ServerSocketFactory.INSTANCE,\n  )\n\n  private val broker: Option[BrokerServer] = if (config.processRoles.contains(ProcessRole.BrokerRole)) {\n    Some(new BrokerServer(sharedServer))\n  } else {\n    None\n  }\n\n  private val controller: Option[ControllerServer] = if (config.processRoles.contains(ProcessRole.ControllerRole)) {\n    Some(new ControllerServer(\n      sharedServer,\n      KafkaRaftServer.configSchema,\n      bootstrapMetadata,\n    ))\n  } else {\n    None\n  }\n\n  override def startup(): Unit = {\n    Mx4jLoader.maybeLoad()\n    // Controller component must be started before the broker component so that\n    // the controller endpoints are passed to the KRaft manager\n    controller.foreach(_.startup())\n    broker.foreach(_.startup())\n    AppInfoParser.registerAppInfo(Server.MetricsPrefix, config.brokerId.toString, metrics, time.milliseconds())\n    info(KafkaBroker.STARTED_MESSAGE)\n  }\n\n  override def shutdown(): Unit = {\n    // In combined mode, we want to shut down the broker first, since the controller may be\n    // needed for controlled shutdown. Additionally, the controller shutdown process currently\n    // stops the raft client early on, which would disrupt broker shutdown.\n    broker.foreach(_.shutdown())\n    controller.foreach(_.shutdown())\n    CoreUtils.swallow(AppInfoParser.unregisterAppInfo(Server.MetricsPrefix, config.brokerId.toString, metrics), this)\n  }\n\n  override def awaitShutdown(): Unit = {\n    broker.foreach(_.awaitShutdown())\n    controller.foreach(_.awaitShutdown())\n  }\n}\n\nobject KafkaRaftServer {\n  val MetadataTopic = Topic.CLUSTER_METADATA_TOPIC_NAME\n  val MetadataPartition = Topic.CLUSTER_METADATA_TOPIC_PARTITION\n  val MetadataTopicId = Uuid.METADATA_TOPIC_ID\n\n  /**\n   * Initialize the configured log directories, including both [[KRaftConfigs.MetadataLogDirProp]]\n   * and [[KafkaConfig.LOG_DIR_PROP]]. This method performs basic validation to ensure that all\n   * directories are accessible and have been initialized with consistent `meta.properties`.\n   *\n   * @param config The process configuration\n   * @return A tuple containing the loaded meta properties (which are guaranteed to\n   *         be consistent across all log dirs) and the offline directories\n   */\n  def initializeLogDirs(\n    config: KafkaConfig,\n    log: Logger,\n    logPrefix: String\n  ): (MetaPropertiesEnsemble, BootstrapMetadata) = {\n    // Load and verify the original ensemble.\n    val loader = new MetaPropertiesEnsemble.Loader()\n    loader.addMetadataLogDir(config.metadataLogDir)\n          .addLogDirs(config.logDirs)\n    val initialMetaPropsEnsemble = loader.load()\n    val verificationFlags = util.EnumSet.of(REQUIRE_AT_LEAST_ONE_VALID, REQUIRE_METADATA_LOG_DIR)\n    initialMetaPropsEnsemble.verify(Optional.empty(), OptionalInt.of(config.nodeId), verificationFlags)\n\n    // Check that the __cluster_metadata-0 topic does not appear outside the metadata directory.\n    val metadataPartitionDirName = UnifiedLog.logDirName(MetadataPartition)\n    initialMetaPropsEnsemble.logDirProps().keySet().forEach(logDir => {\n      if (!logDir.equals(config.metadataLogDir)) {\n        val clusterMetadataTopic = new File(logDir, metadataPartitionDirName)\n        if (clusterMetadataTopic.exists) {\n          throw new KafkaException(s\"Found unexpected metadata location in data directory `$clusterMetadataTopic` \" +\n            s\"(the configured metadata directory is ${config.metadataLogDir}).\")\n        }\n      }\n    })\n\n    // Set directory IDs on all directories. Rewrite the files if needed.\n    val metaPropsEnsemble = {\n      val copier = new MetaPropertiesEnsemble.Copier(initialMetaPropsEnsemble)\n      initialMetaPropsEnsemble.nonFailedDirectoryProps().forEachRemaining(e => {\n        val logDir = e.getKey\n        val metaProps = e.getValue\n        if (!metaProps.isPresent()) {\n          throw new RuntimeException(s\"No `meta.properties` found in $logDir (have you run `kafka-storage.sh` \" +\n            \"to format the directory?)\")\n        }\n        if (!metaProps.get().nodeId().isPresent()) {\n          throw new RuntimeException(s\"Error: node ID not found in $logDir\")\n        }\n        if (!metaProps.get().clusterId().isPresent()) {\n          throw new RuntimeException(s\"Error: cluster ID not found in $logDir\")\n        }\n        val builder = new MetaProperties.Builder(metaProps.get())\n        if (!builder.directoryId().isPresent()) {\n          builder.setDirectoryId(copier.generateValidDirectoryId())\n        }\n        copier.setLogDirProps(logDir, builder.build())\n        copier.setPreWriteHandler((logDir, _, _) => {\n          log.info(\"{}Rewriting {}{}meta.properties\", logPrefix, logDir, File.separator)\n        })\n      })\n      copier.writeLogDirChanges()\n      copier.copy()\n    }\n\n    // Load the BootstrapMetadata.\n    val bootstrapDirectory = new BootstrapDirectory(config.metadataLogDir)\n    val bootstrapMetadata = bootstrapDirectory.read()\n    (metaPropsEnsemble, bootstrapMetadata)\n  }\n\n  val configSchema = new KafkaConfigSchema(Map(\n    ConfigResource.Type.BROKER -> new ConfigDef(KafkaConfig.configDef),\n    ConfigResource.Type.TOPIC -> LogConfig.configDefCopy,\n  ).asJava, ServerTopicConfigSynonyms.ALL_TOPIC_CONFIG_SYNONYMS)\n}\n","numLines":194,"startLine":1,"totalLines":194}}}

implements a comprehensive service lifecycle pattern using a Server interface and trait hierarchy. The core pattern is defined in Server.scala which establishes the Startable/Stoppable lifecycle interface with methods: startup(), shutdown(), and awaitShutdown(). The interface also defines a ProcessStatus enum with states: SHUTDOWN, STARTING, STARTED, and SHUTTING_DOWN.\\n\\nKafkaRaftServer (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaRaftServer.scala) is the top-level entry point that orchestrates the startup and shutdown of both BrokerServer and ControllerServer. In the startup() method, it follows a precise ordering: the controller is started before the broker (line 90-98) to ensure controller endpoints are available. For shutdown, the broker is stopped first (line 104), then the controller, enabling controlled shutdown scenarios.\\n\\nBrokerServer (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/BrokerServer.scala) implements complex startup orchestration starting at line 189. It manages numerous dependent services in order: KafkaScheduler, SocketServer, LogManager, ReplicaManager, TransactionCoordinator, GroupCoordinator, ShareCoordinator, and various other managers. The shutdown() method (line 729) carefully stops services in reverse dependency order: request handlers first, then schedulers, coordinators, replicaManager, logManager, socketServer, and finally lifecycle managers.\\n\\nControllerServer (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ControllerServer.scala) implements a similar pattern starting at line 123. During startup, it initializes metadata cache, publishers, QuorumController, and socket server.
